### 2.3 Espacements & Grille

```css
/* SYSTÃˆME D'ESPACEMENT (Base 4px) */
:root {
  --space-0: 0;
  --space-0.5: 2px;
  --space-1: 4px;
  --space-1.5: 6px;
  --space-2: 8px;
  --space-2.5: 10px;
  --space-3: 12px;
  --space-3.5: 14px;
  --space-4: 16px;
  --space-5: 20px;
  --space-6: 24px;
  --space-7: 28px;
  --space-8: 32px;
  --space-9: 36px;
  --space-10: 40px;
  --space-11: 44px;
  --space-12: 48px;
  --space-14: 56px;
  --space-16: 64px;
  --space-20: 80px;
  --space-24: 96px;
  --space-28: 112px;
  --space-32: 128px;
}

/* CONTENEURS */
.container {
  max-width: 1280px;  /* max-w-7xl */
  margin: 0 auto;
  padding-left: 16px;   /* Mobile: px-4 */
  padding-right: 16px;
}

@media (min-width: 640px) {
  .container {
    padding-left: 24px;  /* sm:px-6 */
    padding-right: 24px;
  }
}

@media (min-width: 1024px) {
  .container {
    padding-left: 32px;  /* lg:px-8 */
    padding-right: 32px;
  }
}

/* GRILLE RESPONSIVE */
.grid-landing {
  display: grid;
  gap: 24px;  /* gap-6 */
  grid-template-columns: 1fr;  /* Mobile: 1 colonne */
}

@media (min-width: 768px) {
  .grid-landing {
    grid-template-columns: repeat(2, 1fr);  /* md: 2 colonnes */
  }
}

@media (min-width: 1024px) {
  .grid-landing {
    grid-template-columns: repeat(3, 1fr);  /* lg: 3 colonnes */
    gap: 32px;
  }
}
```

### 2.4 Bordures & Ombres

```css
/* BORDER RADIUS */
:root {
  --radius-none: 0;
  --radius-sm: 4px;      /* rounded-sm - petits Ã©lÃ©ments */
  --radius-md: 6px;      /* rounded-md - boutons secondaires */
  --radius-lg: 8px;      /* rounded-lg - cartes, inputs */
  --radius-xl: 12px;     /* rounded-xl - grandes cartes */
  --radius-2xl: 16px;    /* rounded-2xl - modales, hero */
  --radius-3xl: 24px;    /* rounded-3xl - Ã©lÃ©ments spÃ©ciaux */
  --radius-full: 9999px; /* rounded-full - badges, avatars */
}

/* OMBRES */
:root {
  --shadow-sm: 0 1px 2px 0 rgba(0, 0, 0, 0.05);
  --shadow-md: 0 4px 6px -1px rgba(0, 0, 0, 0.1),
               0 2px 4px -2px rgba(0, 0, 0, 0.1);
  --shadow-lg: 0 10px 15px -3px rgba(0, 0, 0, 0.1),
               0 4px 6px -4px rgba(0, 0, 0, 0.1);
  --shadow-xl: 0 20px 25px -5px rgba(0, 0, 0, 0.1),
               0 8px 10px -6px rgba(0, 0, 0, 0.1);
  --shadow-2xl: 0 25px 50px -12px rgba(0, 0, 0, 0.25);

  /* Ombre colorÃ©e pour CTA */
  --shadow-red: 0 4px 14px 0 rgba(220, 38, 38, 0.39);
}

/* BORDURES */
:root {
  --border-width: 1px;
  --border-width-2: 2px;
  --border-color: #e5e7eb;        /* gray-200 */
  --border-color-dark: #d1d5db;   /* gray-300 */
  --border-focus: #dc2626;        /* red-600 */
}
```

### 2.7 Animations & Transitions

```css
/* TRANSITIONS STANDARD */
:root {
  --transition-fast: 150ms ease-in-out;
  --transition-base: 200ms ease-in-out;
  --transition-slow: 300ms ease-in-out;
  --transition-slower: 500ms ease-in-out;
}

/* CLASSES TAILWIND */
.transition-colors { transition-property: color, background-color, border-color; }
.transition-transform { transition-property: transform; }
.transition-all { transition-property: all; }
.duration-150 { transition-duration: 150ms; }
.duration-200 { transition-duration: 200ms; }
.duration-300 { transition-duration: 300ms; }
.ease-in-out { transition-timing-function: cubic-bezier(0.4, 0, 0.2, 1); }

/* ANIMATIONS KEYFRAMES */
@keyframes fadeIn {
  from { opacity: 0; }
  to { opacity: 1; }
}

@keyframes slideUp {
  from { opacity: 0; transform: translateY(20px); }
  to { opacity: 1; transform: translateY(0); }
}

@keyframes slideInRight {
  from { opacity: 0; transform: translateX(20px); }
  to { opacity: 1; transform: translateX(0); }
}

@keyframes pulse {
  0%, 100% { opacity: 1; }
  50% { opacity: 0.5; }
}

@keyframes bounce {
  0%, 100% { transform: translateY(-5%); }
  50% { transform: translateY(0); }
}

@keyframes spin {
  from { transform: rotate(0deg); }
  to { transform: rotate(360deg); }
}

/* CLASSES D'ANIMATION */
.animate-fade-in { animation: fadeIn 0.5s ease-out; }
.animate-slide-up { animation: slideUp 0.3s ease-out; }
.animate-pulse { animation: pulse 2s infinite; }
.animate-bounce { animation: bounce 1s infinite; }
.animate-spin { animation: spin 1s linear infinite; }

/* MICRO-INTERACTIONS */
.btn-hover-lift {
  transition: transform 0.2s ease, box-shadow 0.2s ease;
}
.btn-hover-lift:hover {
  transform: translateY(-2px);
  box-shadow: var(--shadow-lg);
}

.btn-press {
  transition: transform 0.1s ease;
}
.btn-press:active {
  transform: scale(0.98);
}
```

### 2.8 Dark Mode

```css
/* VARIABLES DARK MODE */
:root {
  /* Light mode (default) */
  --bg-primary: #ffffff;
  --bg-secondary: #f9fafb;
  --bg-tertiary: #f3f4f6;
  --text-primary: #111827;
  --text-secondary: #6b7280;
  --border-color: #e5e7eb;
}

html.dark {
  /* Dark mode */
  --bg-primary: #111827;
  --bg-secondary: #1f2937;
  --bg-tertiary: #374151;
  --text-primary: #f9fafb;
  --text-secondary: #d1d5db;
  --border-color: #374151;
}

/* OU via media query (prÃ©fÃ©rence systÃ¨me) */
@media (prefers-color-scheme: dark) {
  :root {
    --bg-primary: #111827;
    --bg-secondary: #1f2937;
    --bg-tertiary: #374151;
    --text-primary: #f9fafb;
    --text-secondary: #d1d5db;
    --border-color: #374151;
  }
}

/* CLASSES TAILWIND DARK MODE */
/* Utiliser le prÃ©fixe dark: */
.card {
  @apply bg-white dark:bg-gray-800;
  @apply border-gray-200 dark:border-gray-700;
  @apply text-gray-900 dark:text-gray-100;
}
```

## 3. ARCHITECTURE TECHNIQUE

### 3.1 Stack Technique

```
Frontend:
â”œâ”€â”€ React 18+ avec Suspense
â”œâ”€â”€ TypeScript strict mode
â”œâ”€â”€ Tailwind CSS + CSS Variables (dark mode)
â”œâ”€â”€ Framer Motion (animations)
â”œâ”€â”€ React Hook Form + Zod (validation)
â””â”€â”€ i18next (internationalisation)

Performance:
â”œâ”€â”€ Next.js App Router (SSR/SSG)
â”œâ”€â”€ Image optimization (WebP/AVIF + srcset)
â”œâ”€â”€ Font optimization (variable fonts + font-display: swap)
â”œâ”€â”€ Code splitting par route
â”œâ”€â”€ Lazy loading (Intersection Observer)
â””â”€â”€ Service Worker (PWA offline)

Analytics:
â”œâ”€â”€ Google Analytics 4
â”œâ”€â”€ Hotjar/Clarity (heatmaps)
â”œâ”€â”€ A/B Testing (GrowthBook ou Optimizely)
â””â”€â”€ Core Web Vitals monitoring
```

### 3.3 URLs Structure

```
Pattern: /{locale}-{country}/become-{role}

Exemples:
â”œâ”€â”€ /fr-fr/devenir-avocat-partenaire     (France, FranÃ§ais)
â”œâ”€â”€ /en-gb/become-partner-lawyer          (UK, Anglais)
â”œâ”€â”€ /es-es/convertirse-abogado-socio      (Espagne, Espagnol)
```

## 6. MOBILE-FIRST DESIGN SYSTEM

### 6.1 Breakpoints

```css
/* Mobile First - Base styles are mobile */
:root {
  /* Breakpoints */
  --bp-sm: 640px;   /* Large phones */
  --bp-md: 768px;   /* Tablets */
  --bp-lg: 1024px;  /* Laptops */
  --bp-xl: 1280px;  /* Desktops */
  --bp-2xl: 1536px; /* Large desktops */
}

/* Usage */
.component {
  /* Mobile styles first (default) */
  padding: 16px;
  font-size: 16px;
}

@media (min-width: 768px) {
  .component {
    /* Tablet+ styles */
    padding: 24px;
    font-size: 18px;
  }
}

@media (min-width: 1024px) {
  .component {
    /* Desktop+ styles */
    padding: 32px;
    font-size: 20px;
  }
}
```

### 6.3 Touch Targets

```css
/* Minimum touch target size */
.touch-target {
  min-width: 48px;
  min-height: 48px;
  padding: 12px;
}

/* Spacing between touch targets */
.touch-target + .touch-target {
  margin-left: 8px; /* Minimum 8px gap */
}

/* Button sizes */
.btn-primary {
  min-height: 56px; /* Comfortable for thumbs */
  padding: 16px 32px;
  font-size: 18px;
  font-weight: 600;
}

.btn-secondary {
  min-height: 48px;
  padding: 12px 24px;
  font-size: 16px;
}
```

### 6.4 Sticky Mobile CTA

```tsx
// components/StickyMobileCTA.tsx
interface StickyMobileCTAProps {
  text: string;
  onClick: () => void;
  showAfterScroll?: number; // pixels
}

export const StickyMobileCTA: React.FC<StickyMobileCTAProps> = ({
  text,
  onClick,
  showAfterScroll = 300
}) => {
  const [isVisible, setIsVisible] = useState(false);

  useEffect(() => {
    const handleScroll = () => {
      setIsVisible(window.scrollY > showAfterScroll);
    };
    window.addEventListener('scroll', handleScroll, { passive: true });
    return () => window.removeEventListener('scroll', handleScroll);
  }, [showAfterScroll]);

  return (
    <div
      className={cn(
        "fixed bottom-0 left-0 right-0 z-[9999]",
        "p-4 bg-white border-t border-gray-200",
        "pb-[calc(1rem+env(safe-area-inset-bottom))]", // iPhone notch
        "md:hidden", // Desktop: hidden
        "transform transition-transform duration-300",
        isVisible ? "translate-y-0" : "translate-y-full"
      )}
    >
      <button
        onClick={onClick}
        className="w-full btn-primary"
      >
        {text}
      </button>
    </div>
  );
};
```

### 6.5 Responsive Components Patterns

```tsx
// Pattern 1: Stack on mobile, row on desktop
<div className="flex flex-col md:flex-row gap-4">
  <Card />
  <Card />
  <Card />
</div>

// Pattern 2: 1 column mobile, 2 tablet, 3 desktop
<div className="grid grid-cols-1 md:grid-cols-2 lg:grid-cols-3 gap-6">
  <Card />
  <Card />
  <Card />
</div>

// Pattern 3: Hide on mobile, show on desktop
<div className="hidden md:block">
  Desktop only content
</div>

// Pattern 4: Show on mobile, hide on desktop
<div className="block md:hidden">
  Mobile only content
</div>

// Pattern 5: Different content per breakpoint
<>
  <MobileHero className="md:hidden" />
  <DesktopHero className="hidden md:block" />
</>
```

### 6.6 Performance Mobile

```typescript
// Lazy loading images
<img
  src={placeholder}
  data-src={actualImage}
  loading="lazy"
  decoding="async"
  alt="Description"
/>

// Responsive images
<picture>
  <source
    media="(max-width: 640px)"
    srcSet="/images/hero-mobile.webp"
    type="image/webp"
  />
  <source
    media="(min-width: 641px)"
    srcSet="/images/hero-desktop.webp"
    type="image/webp"
  />
  <img
    src="/images/hero-fallback.jpg"
    alt="Hero"
    loading="eager" // Above the fold
  />
</picture>

// Critical CSS inline
<style dangerouslySetInnerHTML={{
  __html: `
    /* Critical above-the-fold CSS */
    .hero { ... }
    .cta-primary { ... }
  `
}} />
```

### 7.1 Schema Markup FAQPage

```typescript
// utils/schemaMarkup.ts

interface FAQItem {
  question: string;
  answer: string;
}

export function generateFAQSchema(faqs: FAQItem[]): string {
  const schema = {
    "@context": "https://schema.org",
    "@type": "FAQPage",
    "mainEntity": faqs.map(faq => ({
      "@type": "Question",
      "name": faq.question,
      "acceptedAnswer": {
        "@type": "Answer",
        "text": faq.answer
      }
    }))
  };

  return JSON.stringify(schema);
}

// Usage in page
<script
  type="application/ld+json"
  dangerouslySetInnerHTML={{
    __html: generateFAQSchema(faqData)
  }}
/>
```

### 7.3 Meta Tags OptimisÃ©s

```typescript
// components/SEOHead.tsx

interface SEOProps {
  title: string;
  description: string;
  canonicalUrl: string;
  locale: string;
  alternateLocales: { locale: string; url: string }[];
  ogImage?: string;
}

export const SEOHead: React.FC<SEOProps> = ({
  title,
  description,
  canonicalUrl,
  locale,
  alternateLocales,
  ogImage = '/og-default.jpg'
}) => {
  return (
    <Head>
      {/* Primary Meta Tags */}
      <title>{title}</title>
      <meta name="title" content={title} />
      <meta name="description" content={description} />
      <meta name="robots" content="index, follow" />

      {/* Canonical & Hreflang */}
      <link rel="canonical" href={canonicalUrl} />
      {alternateLocales.map(alt => (
        <link
          key={alt.locale}
          rel="alternate"
          hrefLang={alt.locale}
          href={alt.url}
        />
      ))}
      <link rel="alternate" hrefLang="x-default" href={alternateLocales[0]?.url} />

      {/* Open Graph / Facebook */}
      <meta property="og:type" content="website" />
      <meta property="og:url" content={canonicalUrl} />
      <meta property="og:title" content={title} />
      <meta property="og:description" content={description} />
      <meta property="og:image" content={ogImage} />
      <meta property="og:locale" content={locale} />

      {/* Twitter */}
      <meta property="twitter:card" content="summary_large_image" />
      <meta property="twitter:url" content={canonicalUrl} />
      <meta property="twitter:title" content={title} />
      <meta property="twitter:description" content={description} />
      <meta property="twitter:image" content={ogImage} />

      {/* Mobile */}
      <meta name="viewport" content="width=device-width, initial-scale=1, viewport-fit=cover" />
      <meta name="theme-color" content="#1a56db" />
    </Head>
  );
};
```

### 7.4 Structured Data Complet

```typescript
// utils/structuredData.ts

export function generateOrganizationSchema() {
  return {
    "@context": "https://schema.org",
    "@type": "Organization",
    "name": "SOS Expat",
    "url": "https://sosexpat.com",
    "logo": "https://sosexpat.com/logo.png",
    "sameAs": [
      "https://twitter.com/sosexpat",
      "https://linkedin.com/company/sosexpat",
      "https://facebook.com/sosexpat"
    ],
    "contactPoint": {
      "@type": "ContactPoint",
      "telephone": "+33-1-XX-XX-XX-XX",
      "contactType": "customer service",
      "availableLanguage": ["French", "English", "Spanish", "German", "Portuguese", "Arabic", "Chinese", "Hindi", "Russian"]
    }
  };
}

export function generateServiceSchema(locale: string) {
  const services = {
    fr: {
      name: "Mise en relation avocats-expatriÃ©s",
      description: "Plateforme de mise en relation entre avocats spÃ©cialisÃ©s et expatriÃ©s du monde entier"
    },
    en: {
      name: "Lawyer-Expat Matching Service",
      description: "Platform connecting specialized lawyers with expatriates worldwide"
    }
    // ... autres langues
  };

  return {
    "@context": "https://schema.org",
    "@type": "Service",
    "name": services[locale]?.name || services.en.name,
    "description": services[locale]?.description || services.en.description,
    "provider": {
      "@type": "Organization",
      "name": "SOS Expat"
    },
    "areaServed": {
      "@type": "Country",
      "name": "Worldwide"
    }
  };
}

export function generateBreadcrumbSchema(items: { name: string; url: string }[]) {
  return {
    "@context": "https://schema.org",
    "@type": "BreadcrumbList",
    "itemListElement": items.map((item, index) => ({
      "@type": "ListItem",
      "position": index + 1,
      "name": item.name,
      "item": item.url
    }))
  };
}
```

### 7.5 AEO - Answer Engine Optimization (Optimisation pour IA)

```
â”Œâ”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”
â”‚ QU'EST-CE QUE L'AEO ?                                                                        â”‚
```

#### 7.5.4 Schema.org Enrichi pour AEO

```typescript
// utils/aeoSchema.ts

export function generateAEOArticleSchema(article: {
  title: string;
  description: string;
  author: string;
  datePublished: string;
  dateModified: string;
  url: string;
}) {
  return {
    "@context": "https://schema.org",
    "@type": "Article",
    "headline": article.title,
    "description": article.description,
    "author": {
      "@type": "Organization",
      "name": "SOS Expat",
      "url": "https://sosexpat.com",
      "logo": "https://sosexpat.com/logo.png"
    },
    "publisher": {
      "@type": "Organization",
      "name": "SOS Expat",
      "logo": {
        "@type": "ImageObject",
        "url": "https://sosexpat.com/logo.png"
      }
    },
    "datePublished": article.datePublished,
    "dateModified": article.dateModified,
    "mainEntityOfPage": {
      "@type": "WebPage",
      "@id": article.url
    },
    "isAccessibleForFree": true,
    "speakable": {
      "@type": "SpeakableSpecification",
      "cssSelector": ["h1", ".faq-answer", ".key-stats"]
    }
  };
}

export function generateHowToSchema(steps: { name: string; text: string; image?: string }[]) {
  return {
    "@context": "https://schema.org",
    "@type": "HowTo",
    "name": "Comment devenir avocat partenaire SOS Expat",
    "description": "Guide Ã©tape par Ã©tape pour rejoindre le rÃ©seau d'avocats SOS Expat",
    "totalTime": "PT20M",
    "estimatedCost": {
      "@type": "MonetaryAmount",
      "currency": "EUR",
      "value": "0"
    },
    "step": steps.map((step, index) => ({
      "@type": "HowToStep",
      "position": index + 1,
      "name": step.name,
      "text": step.text,
      "image": step.image
    }))
  };
}
```

#### 7.6.2 Checklist Contenu OptimisÃ© IA

```
â–¡ STRUCTURE
  â–¡ H1 unique contenant le mot-clÃ© principal

  â–¡ Pas de saut de niveau (H1 â†’ H3 interdit)

â–¡ RÃ‰PONSES DIRECTES
  â–¡ PremiÃ¨re phrase de chaque section = rÃ©ponse Ã  une question
  â–¡ Format "Question implicite â†’ RÃ©ponse"
  â–¡ Longueur snippet : 40-60 mots
  â–¡ Pas de "Dans cet article, nous allons..."

â–¡ DONNÃ‰ES
  â–¡ Chiffres prÃ©cis (pas "beaucoup", "souvent")
  â–¡ Sources citÃ©es
  â–¡ Date de mise Ã  jour visible
  â–¡ Statistiques vÃ©rifiables

â–¡ LISTES
  â–¡ Ã‰tapes numÃ©rotÃ©es pour les processus
  â–¡ Listes Ã  puces pour les caractÃ©ristiques
  â–¡ Maximum 7 items par liste (mÃ©moire)

â–¡ TABLEAUX
  â–¡ Comparaisons en tableau
  â–¡ Headers clairs
  â–¡ Cellules concises

â–¡ SCHEMA MARKUP
  â–¡ FAQPage pour toutes les FAQ
  â–¡ HowTo pour les tutoriels
  â–¡ Article avec author et dateModified
  â–¡ Organization avec aggregateRating

â–¡ MISE Ã€ JOUR
  â–¡ Date "DerniÃ¨re mise Ã  jour" visible
  â–¡ Contenu actualisÃ© trimestriellement
  â–¡ Statistiques actualisÃ©es mensuellement
```

| MÃ©trique | Outil de Mesure | Objectif |

### 7.8 Optimisations Techniques SEO

```typescript
// next.config.js - Configuration SEO optimale

module.exports = {
  // GÃ©nÃ©ration statique pour les landing pages
  output: 'export',

  // Images optimisÃ©es
  images: {
    formats: ['image/avif', 'image/webp'],
    deviceSizes: [640, 750, 828, 1080, 1200, 1920],
    imageSizes: [16, 32, 48, 64, 96, 128, 256, 384],
  },

  // Headers SEO
  async headers() {
    return [
      {
        source: '/:path*',
        headers: [
          {
            key: 'X-Robots-Tag',
            value: 'index, follow, max-image-preview:large, max-snippet:-1, max-video-preview:-1',
          },
        ],
      },
    ];
  },

  // Redirections SEO (anciennes URLs)
  async redirects() {
    return [
      {
        source: '/avocat-partenaire',
        destination: '/fr-fr/devenir-avocat-partenaire',
        permanent: true, // 301
      },
    ];
  },
};
```

```typescript
// robots.txt dynamique
// pages/robots.txt.tsx

export async function getServerSideProps({ res }) {
  const robotsTxt = `
User-agent: *
Allow: /

# Sitemaps
Sitemap: https://sosexpat.com/sitemap.xml
Sitemap: https://sosexpat.com/sitemap-fr.xml
Sitemap: https://sosexpat.com/sitemap-en.xml
Sitemap: https://sosexpat.com/sitemap-es.xml
Sitemap: https://sosexpat.com/sitemap-de.xml
Sitemap: https://sosexpat.com/sitemap-pt.xml
Sitemap: https://sosexpat.com/sitemap-ar.xml
Sitemap: https://sosexpat.com/sitemap-zh.xml
Sitemap: https://sosexpat.com/sitemap-hi.xml
Sitemap: https://sosexpat.com/sitemap-ru.xml

# Crawl-delay
Crawl-delay: 1

# Disallow
Disallow: /api/
Disallow: /admin/
Disallow: /_next/
Disallow: /private/
`;

  res.setHeader('Content-Type', 'text/plain');
  res.write(robotsTxt);
  res.end();

  return { props: {} };
}

export default function Robots() {
  return null;
}
```

### 8.4 RTL Support (Arabe, HÃ©breu)

```css
/* RTL Global Styles */
[dir="rtl"] {
  /* Flip layout */
  direction: rtl;
  text-align: right;
}

[dir="rtl"] .flex-row {
  flex-direction: row-reverse;
}

[dir="rtl"] .ml-4 {
  margin-left: 0;
  margin-right: 1rem;
}

[dir="rtl"] .mr-4 {
  margin-right: 0;
  margin-left: 1rem;
}

[dir="rtl"] .pl-4 {
  padding-left: 0;
  padding-right: 1rem;
}

[dir="rtl"] .pr-4 {
  padding-right: 0;
  padding-left: 1rem;
}

/* Icons that need flipping */
[dir="rtl"] .icon-arrow-right {
  transform: scaleX(-1);
}

[dir="rtl"] .icon-chevron-left {
  transform: scaleX(-1);
}
```

```tsx
// components/RTLProvider.tsx
import { useLocale } from '@/hooks/useLocale';

export const RTLProvider: React.FC<{ children: React.ReactNode }> = ({ children }) => {
  const { isRTL } = useLocale();

  useEffect(() => {
    document.documentElement.dir = isRTL ? 'rtl' : 'ltr';
    document.documentElement.lang = locale;
  }, [isRTL, locale]);

  return <>{children}</>;
};
```

### 9.2 Cookie Consent Banner

```tsx
// components/CookieConsent.tsx

interface CookieConsentProps {
  locale: string;
}

export const CookieConsent: React.FC<CookieConsentProps> = ({ locale }) => {
  const [showBanner, setShowBanner] = useState(false);
  const [preferences, setPreferences] = useState({
    necessary: true, // Toujours actif
    analytics: false,
    marketing: false,
    preferences: false
  });

  useEffect(() => {
    const consent = localStorage.getItem('cookie-consent');
    if (!consent) {
      setShowBanner(true);
    }
  }, []);

  const handleAcceptAll = () => {
    setPreferences({
      necessary: true,
      analytics: true,
      marketing: true,
      preferences: true
    });
    saveConsent({ ...preferences, analytics: true, marketing: true, preferences: true });
  };

  const handleAcceptNecessary = () => {
    saveConsent(preferences);
  };

  const handleCustomize = () => {
    // Ouvrir modal de personnalisation
  };

  return showBanner ? (
    <div className="fixed bottom-0 left-0 right-0 z-[10000] bg-white border-t shadow-lg p-4 md:p-6">
      <div className="max-w-6xl mx-auto">
        <div className="flex flex-col md:flex-row md:items-center gap-4">
          <div className="flex-1">
            <h3 className="font-semibold text-lg mb-2">
              {t('cookies.title', locale)}
            </h3>
            <p className="text-sm text-gray-600">
              {t('cookies.description', locale)}
              {' '}
              <a href="/privacy" className="text-primary underline">
                {t('cookies.learnMore', locale)}
              </a>
            </p>
          </div>
          <div className="flex flex-col sm:flex-row gap-2">
            <button
              onClick={handleAcceptNecessary}
              className="btn-secondary"
            >
              {t('cookies.necessaryOnly', locale)}
            </button>
            <button
              onClick={handleCustomize}
              className="btn-secondary"
            >
              {t('cookies.customize', locale)}
            </button>
            <button
              onClick={handleAcceptAll}
              className="btn-primary"
            >
              {t('cookies.acceptAll', locale)}
            </button>
          </div>
        </div>
      </div>
    </div>
  ) : null;
};
```

## 10. COMPOSANTS RÃ‰UTILISABLES

### 10.1 Liste des Composants

| Composant | Description | Props principales |
|-----------|-------------|-------------------|
| `TrustBar` | Barre de confiance haut de page | `reviews`, `countries`, `certification` |
| `HeroSection` | Section hero avec vidÃ©o/image | `headline`, `subheadline`, `cta`, `video` |
| `Calculator` | Calculateur interactif | `type`, `specialties`, `countries` |
| `Benefits` | Grille de bÃ©nÃ©fices | `items`, `columns` |
| `HowItWorks` | Timeline Ã©tapes | `steps`, `orientation` |
| `VideoTestimonial` | TÃ©moignage vidÃ©o | `video`, `quote`, `author` |
| `TestimonialsCarousel` | Carrousel tÃ©moignages | `testimonials`, `autoplay` |
| `ComparisonTable` | Tableau comparatif | `rows`, `headers` |
| `FAQAccordion` | FAQ accordÃ©on | `items`, `schemaMarkup` |
| `Guarantees` | Liste de garanties | `items` |
| `FinalCTA` | CTA de fin de page | `title`, `subtitle`, `button`, `phone` |
| `StickyMobileCTA` | CTA fixe mobile | `text`, `onClick` |
| `CookieConsent` | Banner cookies | `locale` |
| `ChatWidget` | Widget chat IA | `locale`, `context` |
| `SocialProofLive` | Notifications temps rÃ©el | `events` |

### 12.3 Format des URLs par Type

```
# === AVOCATS ===

# Par catÃ©gorie de spÃ©cialitÃ©
/{locale}/avocat/specialite/{category-slug}
Exemple: /fr-fr/avocat/specialite/immigration-travail
Exemple: /en-us/lawyers/specialty/immigration-work

# Par sous-spÃ©cialitÃ©
/{locale}/avocat/specialite/{category-slug}/{subspecialty-slug}
Exemple: /fr-fr/avocat/specialite/immigration-travail/visa-etudiant
Exemple: /en-us/lawyers/specialty/immigration-work/student-visa

# Par pays
/{locale}/avocat/pays/{country-slug}
Exemple: /fr-fr/avocat/pays/emirats-arabes-unis
Exemple: /en-us/lawyers/country/united-arab-emirates

# Combinaison spÃ©cialitÃ© + pays
/{locale}/avocat/specialite/{category-slug}/pays/{country-slug}
Exemple: /fr-fr/avocat/specialite/immigration-travail/pays/emirats-arabes-unis


# === EXPATRIÃ‰S ===

# Par type de service
/{locale}/expatrie/service/{service-slug}
Exemple: /fr-fr/expatrie/service/recherche-logement
Exemple: /en-us/expats/service/housing-search

# Par pays
/{locale}/expatrie/pays/{country-slug}
Exemple: /fr-fr/expatrie/pays/thailande
Exemple: /en-us/expats/country/thailand


# === CLIENTS ===

# Par besoin
/{locale}/besoin/{need-slug}
Exemple: /fr-fr/besoin/divorce-international
Exemple: /en-us/need/international-divorce

# Urgences
/{locale}/urgence/{urgency-slug}
Exemple: /fr-fr/urgence/arrete-police-etranger
Exemple: /en-us/emergency/arrested-abroad


# === ACQUISITION ===

# Programme affiliation
/{locale}/programme-affiliation
Exemple: /fr-fr/programme-affiliation
Exemple: /en-us/affiliate-program
```

## 14. STRUCTURE FIRESTORE & TRACKING

### 14.1 Collection `landing_pages_tracking`

```typescript
// Collection Firestore pour suivre chaque landing page

interface LandingPageTracking {
  id: string;                     // Auto-generated
  type: 'lawyer_specialty' | 'lawyer_subspecialty' | 'lawyer_country'
      | 'expat_service' | 'expat_country' | 'client_need'
      | 'affiliate' | 'business' | 'bloggers' | 'partners';
  code: string;                   // Ex: "IMMI", "FR", "INSTALLATION"
  slug: {
    fr: string;
    en: string;
    es: string;
    de: string;
    pt: string;
    ru: string;
    zh: string;
    ar: string;
    hi: string;
  };
  status: {
    fr: 'pending' | 'draft' | 'review' | 'published';
    en: 'pending' | 'draft' | 'review' | 'published';
    es: 'pending' | 'draft' | 'review' | 'published';
    de: 'pending' | 'draft' | 'review' | 'published';
    pt: 'pending' | 'draft' | 'review' | 'published';
    ru: 'pending' | 'draft' | 'review' | 'published';
    zh: 'pending' | 'draft' | 'review' | 'published';
    ar: 'pending' | 'draft' | 'review' | 'published';
    hi: 'pending' | 'draft' | 'review' | 'published';
  };
  content: {
    fr?: LandingPageContent;
    en?: LandingPageContent;
    es?: LandingPageContent;
    de?: LandingPageContent;
    pt?: LandingPageContent;
    ru?: LandingPageContent;
    zh?: LandingPageContent;
    ar?: LandingPageContent;
    hi?: LandingPageContent;
  };
  seo: {
    fr?: LandingPageSEO;
    en?: LandingPageSEO;
    // ... autres langues
  };
  stats: {
    views: number;
    conversions: number;
    lastUpdated: Timestamp;
  };
  createdAt: Timestamp;
  updatedAt: Timestamp;
}

interface LandingPageContent {
  heroTitle: string;
  heroSubtitle: string;
  heroDescription: string;
  benefits: Array<{
    icon: string;
    title: string;
    description: string;
  }>;
  howItWorks: Array<{
    step: number;
    title: string;
    description: string;
  }>;
  faq: Array<{
    question: string;
    answer: string;
  }>;
  testimonials: string[];           // IDs des tÃ©moignages
  ctaTitle: string;
  ctaDescription: string;
  ctaButtonText: string;
}

interface LandingPageSEO {
  title: string;                    // Max 60 chars
  description: string;              // Max 160 chars
  keywords: string[];
  ogImage: string;
  canonicalUrl: string;
  schema: object;                   // JSON-LD schema
}
```

### 14.2 Collection `landing_pages_progress`

```typescript
// Collection pour suivre l'avancement global

interface LandingPagesProgress {
  id: "global_progress";

  // Compteurs globaux
  totalPages: number;           // 5,283
  publishedPages: number;       // Nombre publiÃ©
  draftPages: number;           // En brouillon
  pendingPages: number;         // En attente

  // Par type
  byType: {
    lawyer_specialty: ProgressByLang;
    lawyer_subspecialty: ProgressByLang;
    lawyer_country: ProgressByLang;
    expat_service: ProgressByLang;
    expat_country: ProgressByLang;
    client_need: ProgressByLang;
    acquisition: ProgressByLang;
  };

  // Par pays (Tier 1 uniquement pour le suivi dÃ©taillÃ©)
  byCountry: {
    [countryCode: string]: {
      lawyerPage: StatusByLang;
      expatPage: StatusByLang;
    };
  };

  // DerniÃ¨re mise Ã  jour
  lastUpdated: Timestamp;
}

interface ProgressByLang {
  fr: { total: number; published: number; draft: number; pending: number };
  en: { total: number; published: number; draft: number; pending: number };
  es: { total: number; published: number; draft: number; pending: number };
  de: { total: number; published: number; draft: number; pending: number };
  pt: { total: number; published: number; draft: number; pending: number };
  ru: { total: number; published: number; draft: number; pending: number };
  zh: { total: number; published: number; draft: number; pending: number };
  ar: { total: number; published: number; draft: number; pending: number };
  hi: { total: number; published: number; draft: number; pending: number };
}

type StatusByLang = {
  fr: 'pending' | 'draft' | 'review' | 'published';
  en: 'pending' | 'draft' | 'review' | 'published';
  es: 'pending' | 'draft' | 'review' | 'published';
  de: 'pending' | 'draft' | 'review' | 'published';
  pt: 'pending' | 'draft' | 'review' | 'published';
  ru: 'pending' | 'draft' | 'review' | 'published';
  zh: 'pending' | 'draft' | 'review' | 'published';
  ar: 'pending' | 'draft' | 'review' | 'published';
  hi: 'pending' | 'draft' | 'review' | 'published';
};
```
